title: ProTable
description: Feature-rich data table with search, filtering, reset, sorting, density toggle, column visibility, and drag-to-sort — powered by TanStack Table and shadcn/ui.
---

<ComponentPreview name="pro-table-docs-demo" previewClassName="min-h-[460px]" />

## Installation

<CodeTabs>

<TabsList>
  <TabsTrigger value="cli">Command</TabsTrigger>
  <TabsTrigger value="manual">Manual</TabsTrigger>
</TabsList>

<TabsContent value="cli">

```bash
npx @draco-china/shadcn-pro add pro-table
```

</TabsContent>

<Steps className="mb-0 pt-2">

<Step>Install the following dependencies:</Step>

```bash
bun add @tanstack/react-table @dnd-kit/core @dnd-kit/sortable @dnd-kit/utilities
```

<Step>Copy and paste the following code into your project.</Step>

<ComponentSource name="pro-table" title="components/pro/pro-table/index.tsx" />

<Step>Update the import paths to match your project setup.</Step>

</Steps>

</TabsContent>

</CodeTabs>

## Usage

```tsx
import { ProTable } from "@/components/pro/pro-table"

const columns = [
  {
    accessorKey: "name",
    header: "Name",
    enableSorting: true,
    meta: { pinned: "left" },
  },
  { accessorKey: "email", header: "Email" },
  { accessorKey: "createdAt", header: "Created", meta: { pinned: "right" } },
]

export default function UsersTable() {
  return (
    <ProTable
      columns={columns}
      data={users}
      searchKey="name"
      searchPlaceholder="Search by name..."
      header={<h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Users</h2>}
      stickyHeader
      onRefresh={() => refetch()}
    />
  )
}
```

## Examples

### Pinned Columns and Sticky Header

Use `meta.pinned` on column definitions to keep important columns visible during horizontal scroll. Users can also pin or unpin columns from the column settings menu. The table header is sticky by default; set `stickyHeader={false}` to disable it.

```tsx
const columns = [
  { id: "select", size: 48, meta: { pinned: "left" } },
  { accessorKey: "name", header: "Name", size: 180, meta: { pinned: "left" } },
  { accessorKey: "email", header: "Email", size: 240 },
  { accessorKey: "createdAt", header: "Created", size: 150, meta: { pinned: "right" } },
]

<ProTable columns={columns} data={users} />
```

### Filtering with Reset

Add `meta.filters` to any column — ProTable **automatically** renders a `FacetedFilter` (Popover + Checkbox) in the toolbar, maps `value → label` in cells, and shows a **Reset** button whenever any filter is active.

- Default mode is **multi-select** — use `filterFn: "multiValueFilter"` (built-in)
- Set `meta.filterMode: "single"` for single-select (radio-like), use `filterFn: "equals"`

<ComponentPreview name="pro-table-filter-demo" previewClassName="min-h-[460px]" />

```tsx
const columns: ColumnDef<User>[] = [
  {
    accessorKey: "role",
    header: "Role",
    filterFn: "multiValueFilter", // built-in, handles string[] filter value
    meta: {
      filterPlaceholder: "Role",
      filters: [
        { label: "Admin", value: "admin" },
        { label: "Editor", value: "editor" },
      ],
    },
  },
  {
    accessorKey: "status",
    header: "Status",
    filterFn: "equals",
    meta: {
      filterPlaceholder: "Status",
      filterMode: "single",   // single-select
      filterVariant: "text",  // cell renders as plain text (default: 'badge')
      filters: [
        { label: "Active", value: "active" },
        { label: "Inactive", value: "inactive" },
      ],
    },
  },
]

// No filterRender needed — FacetedFilters are auto-rendered from meta
<ProTable columns={columns} data={data} searchKey="name" />
```

You can still pass `filterRender` (ReactNode or function) for fully custom controls.

### Bulk Actions

Render bottom-floating bulk actions when rows are selected. The floating toolbar supports keyboard navigation and `Escape` clears the selection.

```tsx
<ProTable
  columns={columns}
  data={users}
  bulkActionEntityName="user"
  bulkActionRender={({ selectedRows }) => (
    <Button size="sm" variant="outline">
      Export {selectedRows.length}
    </Button>
  )}
/>
```

### Drag-to-Sort

Enable row drag-to-sort with the `dragSort` prop. Use `rowKey` to specify the unique identifier field and `onDragSortEnd` to receive the reordered data.

Drag sorting reorders the backing `data` array by the currently rendered rows. When the table is filtered or paginated, the dragged row moves relative to the visible target row in the original data array.

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-table-drag-sort-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[520px]"
/>

```tsx
<ProTable
  columns={columns}
  data={data}
  dragSort
  rowKey="id"
  onDragSortEnd={(newData) => console.log(newData)}
/>
```

## API Reference

### ProTable

| Prop                    | Type                                  | Default                      | Description                                                                                                    |
| ----------------------- | ------------------------------------- | ---------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `columns`               | `ColumnDef<T>[]`                      | —                            | TanStack Table column definitions.                                                                             |
| `data`                  | `T[]`                                 | —                            | Table data array.                                                                                              |
| `header`                | `ReactNode \| (context) => ReactNode` | —                            | Custom content rendered above the toolbar.                                                                     |
| `searchKey`             | `string`                              | —                            | Column key to enable text filtering on.                                                                        |
| `searchPlaceholder`     | `string`                              | `'Search...'`                | Placeholder text for the search input.                                                                         |
| `filterRender`          | `ReactNode \| (table) => ReactNode`   | —                            | Custom filter controls rendered after the auto filters. Pass a function to access the table instance. |
| `filterMode` *(meta)*   | `'single' \| 'multi'`                 | `'multi'`                    | Column meta — selection mode for the auto-rendered FacetedFilter.                                    |
| `filterVariant` *(meta)*| `'badge' \| 'text'`                   | `'badge'`                    | Column meta — cell display style when `meta.filters` is set.                                         |
| `toolBarRender`         | `() => ReactNode[]`                   | —                            | Extra action buttons rendered on the right side of the toolbar.                                                |
| `bulkActionRender`      | `(context) => ReactNode`              | —                            | Actions shown in the bulk toolbar when rows are selected.                                                      |
| `bulkActionEntityName`  | `string`                              | `'row'`                      | Singular entity name used in the bulk toolbar selection count.                                                 |
| `showColumnToggle`      | `boolean`                             | `true`                       | Show the column visibility toggle button.                                                                      |
| `onRefresh`             | `() => void`                          | —                            | Refresh callback — shows a refresh button when provided.                                                       |
| `pageSizeOptions`       | `number[]`                            | `[10,20,50,100]`             | Page size options for the pagination control.                                                                  |
| `dragSort`              | `boolean`                             | `false`                      | Enable row drag-to-sort (disables column header click-to-sort).                                                |
| `rowKey`                | `keyof T`                             | —                            | Unique field used as the drag sort key (falls back to row index).                                              |
| `onDragSortEnd`         | `(newData: T[]) => void`              | —                            | Called after drag sort completes with the reordered data.                                                      |
| `loading`               | `boolean`                             | `false`                      | Shows a skeleton loading state.                                                                                |
| `loadingRows`           | `number`                              | `5`                          | Number of skeleton rows to display.                                                                            |
| `emptyText`             | `ReactNode`                           | `'No data'`                  | Empty state text or custom content.                                                                            |
| `emptyIcon`             | `ReactNode`                           | inbox icon                   | Empty state icon.                                                                                              |
| `showPagination`        | `boolean`                             | `true`                       | Show or hide the built-in pagination bar.                                                                      |
| `layout`                | `'full' \| 'auto'`                    | `'full'`                     | Full layout fills the available height and keeps pagination at the bottom; auto layout follows content height. |
| `stickyHeader`          | `boolean`                             | `true`                       | Keep the table header visible while the table body scrolls.                                                    |
| `columnPinning`         | `ColumnPinningState`                  | from `columns[].meta.pinned` | Controlled column pinning state. Columns can also set `meta: { pinned: 'left' \| 'right' }`.                   |
| `onColumnPinningChange` | `OnChangeFn<ColumnPinningState>`      | —                            | Called when column pinning changes.                                                                            |
| `className`             | `string`                              | —                            | Additional className for the outer container.                                                                  |
| `pagination`            | `ProTablePaginationState`             | internal                     | Controlled pagination state (`{ pageIndex, pageSize, total? }`). `total` is the server-side row count used to compute page count. Pair with `onPaginationChange`. When provided, server-side pagination is assumed. |
| `onPaginationChange`    | `OnChangeFn<ProTablePaginationState>` | —                            | Called when page or page size changes.                                                   |
| `sorting`               | `SortingState`                        | internal                     | Controlled sorting state. Pair with `onSortingChange`. When provided, server-side sorting is assumed. |
| `onSortingChange`       | `OnChangeFn<SortingState>`            | —                            | Called when sort column or direction changes.                                             |
| `columnFilters`         | `ColumnFiltersState`                  | internal                     | Controlled column filters state. Pair with `onColumnFiltersChange`.                      |
| `onColumnFiltersChange` | `OnChangeFn<ColumnFiltersState>`      | —                            | Called when column filters change.                                                       |
| `globalFilter`          | `string`                              | internal                     | Controlled global filter value. Pair with `onGlobalFilterChange`.                        |
| `onGlobalFilterChange`  | `OnChangeFn<string>`                  | —                            | Called when the global filter changes.                                                   |

### useProTableUrlState

Sync pagination, global filter, and column filters to URL search params — framework-agnostic via a `search` + `navigate` interface (compatible with TanStack Router, Next.js App Router, React Router, etc.).

```tsx
import { useProTableUrlState } from '@/components/ui/pro-table/use-pro-table-url-state'

const tableState = useProTableUrlState({
  search: { page: 2, filter: 'alice' },  // current URL search params
  navigate: ({ search }) => { /* push new params to router */ },
})
```

**Parameters:**

| Option          | Type            | Default      | Description                                      |
| --------------- | --------------- | ------------ | ------------------------------------------------ |
| `search`        | `SearchRecord`  | —            | Current URL search params as a plain object.     |
| `navigate`      | `NavigateFn`    | —            | Called with updated params to push to the router.|
| `pagination.pageKey`      | `string` | `'page'`    | URL key for current page.            |
| `pagination.pageSizeKey`  | `string` | `'pageSize'`| URL key for page size.               |
| `pagination.defaultPage`  | `number` | `1`         | Default page (omitted from URL).     |
| `pagination.defaultPageSize` | `number` | `10`     | Default page size (omitted from URL).|
| `globalFilter.enabled`    | `boolean`| `true`      | Enable global filter state.          |
| `globalFilter.key`        | `string` | `'filter'`  | URL key for the global filter.       |
| `columnFilters` | `Array<ColumnFilterConfig>` | `[]`  | Column filter definitions with URL key mapping. |

**Returns:**

| Key                    | Type                          | Description                               |
| ---------------------- | ----------------------------- | ----------------------------------------- |
| `pagination`           | `PaginationState`             | Pass to `<ProTable pagination={...} />`.  |
| `onPaginationChange`   | `OnChangeFn<PaginationState>` | Pass to `<ProTable onPaginationChange={...} />`. |
| `globalFilter`         | `string`                      | Pass to `<ProTable globalFilter={...} />`. |
| `onGlobalFilterChange` | `OnChangeFn<string>`          | Pass to `<ProTable onGlobalFilterChange={...} />`. |
| `columnFilters`        | `ColumnFiltersState`          | Pass to `<ProTable columnFilters={...} />`. |
| `onColumnFiltersChange`| `OnChangeFn<ColumnFiltersState>` | Pass to `<ProTable onColumnFiltersChange={...} />`. |
| `ensurePageInRange`    | `(pageCount: number) => void` | Call after data loads to clamp the page.  |

**Example with Next.js App Router:**

```tsx
'use client'

import { useRouter, useSearchParams } from 'next/navigation'
import { useProTableUrlState } from '@/components/ui/pro-table/use-pro-table-url-state'
import { ProTable } from '@/components/ui/pro-table'

export default function UsersTable() {
  const router = useRouter()
  const searchParams = useSearchParams()

  const search = Object.fromEntries(searchParams.entries())

  const tableState = useProTableUrlState({
    search,
    navigate: ({ search: next }) => {
      const params = new URLSearchParams()
      const resolved = typeof next === 'function' ? next(search) : next
      for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(resolved)) {
        if (v !== undefined) params.set(k, String(v))
      }
      router.push(`?${params.toString()}`)
    },
  })

  return (
    <ProTable
      {...tableState}
      columns={columns}
      data={data}
    />
  )
}
```

6c:T720,"use client"

import type { ColumnDef } from "@tanstack/react-table"
import { ProTable } from "@/components/pro/pro-table/index"

type User = {
  name: string
  email: string
  role: "admin" | "editor" | "viewer"
  status: "active" | "inactive"
}

const data: User[] = [
  { name: "Alice Wang", email: "alice@example.com", role: "admin", status: "active" },
  { name: "Bob Chen", email: "bob@example.com", role: "editor", status: "active" },
  { name: "Carol Liu", email: "carol@example.com", role: "viewer", status: "inactive" },
  { name: "David Zhang", email: "david@example.com", role: "editor", status: "active" },
  { name: "Eve Lin", email: "eve@example.com", role: "admin", status: "inactive" },
  { name: "Frank Wu", email: "frank@example.com", role: "viewer", status: "active" },
]

const columns: ColumnDef<User>[] = [
  { accessorKey: "name", header: "Name" },
  { accessorKey: "email", header: "Email" },
  {
    accessorKey: "role",
    header: "Role",
    filterFn: "multiValueFilter",
    meta: {
      filterPlaceholder: "Role",
      filters: [
        { label: "Admin", value: "admin" },
        { label: "Editor", value: "editor" },
        { label: "Viewer", value: "viewer" },
      ],
    },
  },
  {
    accessorKey: "status",
    header: "Status",
    filterFn: "equals",
    meta: {
      filterPlaceholder: "Status",
      filterVariant: "text",
      filterMode: "single",
      filters: [
        { label: "Active", value: "active" },
        { label: "Inactive", value: "inactive" },
      ],
    },
  },
]

export function ProTableFilterDemo() {
  return (
    <div className="h-[460px] w-full p-4">
      <ProTable
        columns={columns}
        data={data}
        searchKey="name"
        searchPlaceholder="Search by name..."
        pageSizeOptions={[6, 10]}
      />
    </div>
  )
}

8e:T9bc,'use client'

import * as React from 'react'
import { type ColumnDef } from '@tanstack/react-table'
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge'
import { ProTable } from '@/components/pro/pro-table/index'

type Task = {
  id: string
  title: string
  priority: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high'
  status: 'todo' | 'in-progress' | 'done'
}

const initialData: Task[] = [
  { id: '1', title: 'Design system architecture', priority: 'high', status: 'done' },
  { id: '2', title: 'Set up dev environment', priority: 'high', status: 'done' },
  { id: '3', title: 'Implement ProTable component', priority: 'high', status: 'in-progress' },
  { id: '4', title: 'Implement ProForm component', priority: 'medium', status: 'in-progress' },
  { id: '5', title: 'Write unit tests', priority: 'medium', status: 'todo' },
  { id: '6', title: 'Improve documentation site', priority: 'low', status: 'todo' },
  { id: '7', title: 'Publish npm package', priority: 'low', status: 'todo' },
]

const priorityVariant: Record<Task['priority'], 'destructive' | 'default' | 'secondary'> = {
  high: 'destructive',
  medium: 'default',
  low: 'secondary',
}

const priorityLabel: Record<Task['priority'], string> = {
  high: 'High',
  medium: 'Medium',
  low: 'Low',
}

const statusLabel: Record<Task['status'], string> = {
  'todo': 'Todo',
  'in-progress': 'In Progress',
  'done': 'Done',
}

const columns: ColumnDef<Task>[] = [
  { accessorKey: 'title', header: 'Task' },
  {
    accessorKey: 'priority',
    header: 'Priority',
    cell: ({ row }) => (
      <Badge variant={priorityVariant[row.getValue('priority') as Task['priority']]}>
        {priorityLabel[row.getValue('priority') as Task['priority']]}
      </Badge>
    ),
  },
  {
    accessorKey: 'status',
    header: 'Status',
    cell: ({ row }) => (
      <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
        {statusLabel[row.getValue('status') as Task['status']]}
      </span>
    ),
  },
]

export function ProTableDragSortDemo() {
  const [order, setOrder] = React.useState<string[]>([])

  return (
    <div className="h-full w-full space-y-3 p-4">
      <ProTable
        data={initialData}
        columns={columns}
        dragSort
        rowKey="id"
        onDragSortEnd={(newData) => setOrder(newData.map((d) => d.title))}
        pageSizeOptions={[5, 10]}
      />
      {order.length > 0 && (
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground px-1">
          Current order: {order.join(' → ')}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

import {
  closestCenter,
  DndContext,
  type DragEndEvent,
  KeyboardSensor,
  PointerSensor,
  useSensor,
  useSensors,
} from '@dnd-kit/core'
import { sortableKeyboardCoordinates } from '@dnd-kit/sortable'
import {
  type ColumnDef,
  type ColumnFiltersState,
  type ColumnPinningState,
  getCoreRowModel,
  getFacetedRowModel,
  getFacetedUniqueValues,
  getFilteredRowModel,
  getPaginationRowModel,
  getSortedRowModel,
  type OnChangeFn,
  type PaginationState,
  type Row,
  type SortingState,
  type Table as TanStackTable,
  useReactTable,
  type VisibilityState,
} from '@tanstack/react-table'
import * as React from 'react'

import { TableBody, TableHeader } from '@/components/ui/table'

const tableScrollbarClassName =
  '[scrollbar-gutter:auto] [scrollbar-width:thin] [scrollbar-color:transparent_transparent] hover:[scrollbar-color:rgba(148,163,184,0.45)_transparent] [&::-webkit-scrollbar]:h-2 [&::-webkit-scrollbar]:w-2 [&::-webkit-scrollbar-track]:bg-transparent [&::-webkit-scrollbar-track]:shadow-none [&::-webkit-scrollbar-corner]:bg-transparent [&::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb]:rounded-full [&::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb]:border-0 [&::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb]:bg-transparent hover:[&::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb]:bg-muted-foreground/35'

export interface ProTableRenderContext<TData> {
  table: TanStackTable<TData>
  rows: Row<TData>[]
  selectedRows: Row<TData>[]
}

export type ProTableLayout = 'full' | 'auto'

export type ProTablePaginationState = PaginationState & { total?: number }

export interface ProTableProps<TData, TValue> {
  columns: ColumnDef<TData, TValue>[]
  data: TData[]
  header?: React.ReactNode | ((context: ProTableRenderContext<TData>) => React.ReactNode)
  filterRender?: React.ReactNode
  toolBarRender?: () => React.ReactNode[]
  bulkActionRender?: (context: ProTableRenderContext<TData>) => React.ReactNode
  bulkActionEntityName?: string
  searchKey?: string
  searchPlaceholder?: string
  showColumnToggle?: boolean
  onRefresh?: () => void
  pageSizeOptions?: number[]
  dragSort?: boolean
  onDragSortEnd?: (newData: TData[]) => void
  rowKey?: keyof TData
  loading?: boolean
  loadingRows?: number
  emptyText?: React.ReactNode
  emptyIcon?: React.ReactNode
  showPagination?: boolean
  layout?: ProTableLayout
  stickyHeader?: boolean
  columnPinning?: ColumnPinningState
  onColumnPinningChange?: OnChangeFn<ColumnPinningState>
  className?: string
  /** Controlled pagination state. Pair with `onPaginationChange`. When provided, server-side pagination is assumed. */
  pagination?: ProTablePaginationState
  onPaginationChange?: OnChangeFn<ProTablePaginationState>
  /** Controlled sorting state. Pair with `onSortingChange`. When provided, server-side sorting is assumed. */
  sorting?: SortingState
  onSortingChange?: OnChangeFn<SortingState>
  /** Controlled column filters state. Pair with `onColumnFiltersChange`. */
  columnFilters?: ColumnFiltersState
  onColumnFiltersChange?: OnChangeFn<ColumnFiltersState>
  /** Controlled global filter value. Pair with `onGlobalFilterChange`. */
  globalFilter?: string
  onGlobalFilterChange?: OnChangeFn<string>

}

export function ProTable<TData, TValue>({
  columns,
  data: initialData,
  header,
  filterRender,
  toolBarRender,
  bulkActionRender,
  bulkActionEntityName,
  searchKey,
  searchPlaceholder = 'Search...',
  showColumnToggle = true,
  onRefresh,
  pageSizeOptions,
  dragSort = false,
  onDragSortEnd,
  rowKey,
  loading = false,
  loadingRows = 5,
  emptyText = 'No data',
  emptyIcon,
  showPagination = true,
  layout = 'full',
  stickyHeader = true,
  columnPinning,
  onColumnPinningChange,
  className,
  pagination: paginationProp,
  onPaginationChange,
  sorting: sortingProp,
  onSortingChange: onSortingChangeProp,
  columnFilters: columnFiltersProp,
  onColumnFiltersChange: onColumnFiltersChangeProp,
  globalFilter: globalFilterProp,
  onGlobalFilterChange,
}: ProTableProps<TData, TValue>) {
  const [data, setData] = React.useState<TData[]>(initialData)
  const [rowSelection, setRowSelection] = React.useState({})
  const [columnVisibility, setColumnVisibility] = React.useState<VisibilityState>({})
  const [internalColumnFilters, setInternalColumnFilters] = React.useState<ColumnFiltersState>([])
  const columnFilters = columnFiltersProp ?? internalColumnFilters
  const setColumnFilters: OnChangeFn<ColumnFiltersState> = onColumnFiltersChangeProp ?? setInternalColumnFilters
  const [internalGlobalFilter, setInternalGlobalFilter] = React.useState<string>('')
  const globalFilter = globalFilterProp ?? internalGlobalFilter
  const setGlobalFilter: OnChangeFn<string> = onGlobalFilterChange ?? setInternalGlobalFilter
  const [internalSorting, setInternalSorting] = React.useState<SortingState>([])
  const sorting = sortingProp ?? internalSorting
  const setSorting: OnChangeFn<SortingState> = onSortingChangeProp ?? setInternalSorting
  const manualPagination = paginationProp !== undefined
  const manualSorting = onSortingChangeProp !== undefined

  const [internalPagination, setInternalPagination] = React.useState<PaginationState>({
    pageIndex: 0,
    pageSize: 10,
  })
  const pagination = paginationProp ?? internalPagination
  const setPagination: OnChangeFn<ProTablePaginationState> = onPaginationChange ?? setInternalPagination
  const [tableSize, setTableSize] = React.useState<TableSize>('default')
  const defaultColumnOrder = React.useMemo(() => getLeafColumnIds(columns), [columns])
  const defaultColumnPinning = React.useMemo(() => getDefaultColumnPinning(columns), [columns])
  const defaultColumnOrderKey = defaultColumnOrder.join('\0')
  const defaultColumnPinningKey = `${defaultColumnPinning.left?.join('\0') ?? ''}\u0001${defaultColumnPinning.right?.join('\0') ?? ''}`
  const [columnOrder, setColumnOrder] = React.useState<string[]>(defaultColumnOrder)
  const [internalColumnPinning, setInternalColumnPinning] =
    React.useState<ColumnPinningState>(defaultColumnPinning)
  const currentColumnPinning = columnPinning ?? internalColumnPinning

  React.useEffect(() => setData(initialData), [initialData])
  React.useEffect(() => {
    setColumnOrder((current) => [
      ...current.filter((id) => defaultColumnOrder.includes(id)),
      ...defaultColumnOrder.filter((id) => !current.includes(id)),
    ])
  }, [defaultColumnOrderKey])
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (columnPinning) return
    setInternalColumnPinning(defaultColumnPinning)
  }, [columnPinning, defaultColumnPinningKey])

  const handleColumnPinningChange = React.useCallback<OnChangeFn<ColumnPinningState>>(
    (updater) => {
      setInternalColumnPinning(updater)
      onColumnPinningChange?.(updater)
    },
    [onColumnPinningChange],
  )

  const table = useReactTable({
    data,
    columns,
    state: {
      sorting,
      columnVisibility,
      rowSelection,
      columnFilters,
      globalFilter,
      columnOrder,
      columnPinning: currentColumnPinning,
      pagination,
    },
    enableRowSelection: true,
    enableColumnPinning: true,
    onRowSelectionChange: setRowSelection,
    onSortingChange: setSorting,
    onColumnFiltersChange: setColumnFilters,
    onGlobalFilterChange: setGlobalFilter,
    onColumnVisibilityChange: setColumnVisibility,
    onColumnOrderChange: setColumnOrder,
    onColumnPinningChange: handleColumnPinningChange,
    onPaginationChange: setPagination,
    manualPagination,
    manualSorting,
    rowCount: pagination.total,
    getCoreRowModel: getCoreRowModel(),
    getFilteredRowModel: getFilteredRowModel(),
    getPaginationRowModel: getPaginationRowModel(),
    getSortedRowModel: getSortedRowModel(),
    getFacetedRowModel: getFacetedRowModel(),
    getFacetedUniqueValues: getFacetedUniqueValues(),
    getRowId: rowKey
      ? (row) => String((row as Record<string, unknown>)[rowKey as string])
      : undefined,
  })

  const sensors = useSensors(
    useSensor(PointerSensor),
    useSensor(KeyboardSensor, {
      coordinateGetter: sortableKeyboardCoordinates,
    }),
  )

  function handleDragEnd(event: DragEndEvent) {
    const { active, over } = event
    if (!over || active.id === over.id) return

    const nextData = reorderDataByRows(
      data,
      table.getRowModel().rows,
      String(active.id),
      String(over.id),
    )
    if (nextData === data) return

    setData(nextData)
    onDragSortEnd?.(nextData)
  }

  const rows = table.getRowModel().rows
  const rowIds = rows.map((row) => row.id)
  const selectedRows = table.getFilteredSelectedRowModel().rows
  const visibleColumns = table.getVisibleLeafColumns()
  const visibleColumnCount = visibleColumns.length + (dragSort ? 1 : 0)
  const renderContext = React.useMemo<ProTableRenderContext<TData>>(
    () => ({ table, rows, selectedRows }),
    [table, rows, selectedRows],
  )
  const isFullLayout = layout === 'full'
  const headerContent = typeof header === 'function' ? header(renderContext) : header
  const bulkActions = bulkActionRender?.(renderContext)
  const content = (
    <>
      <div
        className={cn(
          'overflow-auto rounded-md border',
          tableScrollbarClassName,
          isFullLayout && 'min-h-0 flex-1',
        )}
      >
        <table data-slot="table" className="w-full min-w-max caption-bottom text-sm">
          <TableHeader>
            <ProTableHeader
              headerGroups={table.getHeaderGroups()}
              dragSort={dragSort}
              sticky={stickyHeader}
            />
          </TableHeader>
          <TableBody>
            <ProTableBody
              rows={rows}
              rowIds={rowIds}
              visibleColumns={visibleColumns}
              visibleColumnCount={visibleColumnCount}
              dragSort={dragSort}
              loading={loading}
              loadingRows={loadingRows}
              paddingClass={cellPadding[tableSize]}
              emptyIcon={emptyIcon}
              emptyText={emptyText}
            />
          </TableBody>
        </table>
      </div>
      {showPagination && (
        <div className={cn(isFullLayout && 'shrink-0')}>
          <ProTablePagination table={table} pageSizeOptions={pageSizeOptions} />
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  )

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(isFullLayout ? 'flex h-full min-h-0 flex-col gap-3' : 'space-y-3', className)}
    >
      {headerContent && <div className="shrink-0">{headerContent}</div>}
      <ProTableToolbar
        table={table}
        disabled={loading}
        filterRender={filterRender}
        toolBarRender={toolBarRender}
        searchKey={searchKey}
        searchPlaceholder={searchPlaceholder}
        showColumnToggle={showColumnToggle}
        onRefresh={onRefresh}
        tableSize={tableSize}
        onTableSizeChange={setTableSize}
        defaultColumnOrder={defaultColumnOrder}
        defaultColumnPinning={defaultColumnPinning}
      />
      {dragSort && !loading ? (
        <DndContext sensors={sensors} collisionDetection={closestCenter} onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}>
          {content}
        </DndContext>
      ) : (
        content
      )}
      {bulkActionRender && (
        <ProTableBulkActions table={table} entityName={bulkActionEntityName}>
          {bulkActions}
        </ProTableBulkActions>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
